# Exploring MS Teams

I'm not able to open the dev tools in the MS Teams app on macOS anymore.

1. Open the desktop app (on windows? macos v below doesn't have new fluent emoji)
2. Grab some emoji from the Preview pane


## macOS

Desktop app uses old version of emoji

> You have Microsoft Teams Version 1.5.00.11157. It was last updated on 2022-06-05.

Doesn't work in Orion or Firefox. Chrome shows old emoji.

If you enable Developer Prview on Chrome, it work!


## Windows

The exp. on Brave doesn't work -- it's still using v1 of the emoji. Trying the
desktop app.

By default, same deal. v1. However, apparently you need the Develoepr Preview.
... > About > Developer Preview > Accept (or whatever

https://statics.teams.cdn.live.net/teams-modular-packages/hashed-assets/services-emoticon-0a3c5aa7f01e93d3.json
https://statics.teams.cdn.live.net/evergreen-assets/personal-expressions/v1/metadata/8479a21d47934aed85d6d6f236847484/en-us.json

Looks like you have to use the preview in the desktop app ATM.

There's a request to `services-emotioncs*.js` which has this source:


Animations are done via PNGs using sprites.

Like this, for example:

[!https://statics.teams.cdn.office.net/evergreen-assets/personal-expressions/v2/assets/emoticons/cwl/default/30_anim_f.png?v16]

The image is 30px wide (and each frame is therefore 30px tall). height / 30px is the number of frames.

60 is also supported:

https://statics.teams.cdn.office.net/evergreen-assets/personal-expressions/v2/assets/emoticons/cwl/default/60_anim_f.png?v16

but 90 and 120 are not.


There's a version tag (`?vX`) but that doesn't seem to make a huge difference?
Would like to pull two files and do a diff at some point.
